## Output Files

- `data/all-pages.json` - Complete page data for all pages
- `data/sitemap.json` - Site structure and meta information
- `data/images.json` - Image metadata and download status
- `data/documents.json` - Downloaded documents list
- `data/contact-info.json` - Emails, phones, social links
- `data/forms.json` - All forms and their fields
- `data/external-links.json` - All external links
- `data/structured-data.json` - JSON-LD structured data
- `data/navigation.json` - Navigation structure
- `data/assets.json` - CSS, JS, and video assets
- `data/manifest.json` - Scraping manifest and statistics
- `images/` - Downloaded images
- `assets/documents/` - Downloaded documents (PDFs, etc.)
